esicolor_formables = {
	highlight_required_states = {
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		visible = {
			has_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected
			NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_EAR_UNITED }
		}
		complete_effect = {
			clr_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected
		}
	}

	highlight_affected_states = {
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_visual }
			NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = formed_EAR_UNITED }
		}
		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected
		}
	}

	#enable_formable_colors = {

	#	}
	#	complete_effect = {

	#disable_formable_colors = {
	#	allowed = {
	#		always = yes
	#	}
	#	visible = {
	#		NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_colors_enabled }

	form_slovenia = {
		icon = generic_form_nation
		allowed = {
			can_form_slovenia = yes
		}
		visible = {
			has_formed_a_formable = no
		}
		available = {
			has_states_to_form_slovenia = yes
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision form_slovenia"
			set_country_flag = can_form_YUG_UNITED
			set_country_flag = can_form_DNB_UNITED

			set_cosmetic_tag = YUG_SLOVENIA

			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_slovenia = yes }

					formable_decision_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_visual } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = form_slovenia_affected_states_tt
				formable_decision_effect_tooltip = yes
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected }

					is_slovenia = yes
				}
				else = {
					required_states_to_form_slovenia = yes
				}
			}
		}

		cost = global.formables_cost_25?25

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5000
		}
	}

			clr_country_flag = can_form_TUR_UNITED
			clr_country_flag = can_form_ROM_UNITED

			set_country_flag = can_form_EUR_UNITED

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = EAI_halife_abdulmecid_efendi ruling_only = yes } }

				set_cosmetic_tag = UBF_UNITED_ABDULMEJID
				EAI_halife_abdulmecid_efendi = { set_character_name = TUR_abdulmejid_ii }

				else = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = UBF_UNITED
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_balkans = yes }

					formable_decision_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_visual } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = form_balkans_affected_states_tt

	form_spain = {
		icon = generic_form_nation
		allowed = {
			can_form_spain = yes
		}
		visible = {
			has_cosmetics_to_form_spain = yes
		}
		available = {
			has_states_to_form_spain = yes
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision form_spain"
			clr_country_flag = can_form_IBR_SPAIN

			set_country_flag = can_form_IBR_UNITED

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = ILS_julian_gorkin ruling_only = yes } }

				set_cosmetic_tag = IBR_SPAIN_POUM
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = IFI_francisco_franco ruling_only = yes } }

				set_cosmetic_tag = IBR_SPAIN_FRANCO
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = IFL_manuel_fal_conde ruling_only = yes } }

				set_cosmetic_tag = IBR_SPAIN_CARLIST
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_ideology = anarchism }

				set_cosmetic_tag = IBR_SPAIN_ANARCHIST
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_ideology = falangism }

				set_cosmetic_tag = IBR_SPAIN_DIRECTORY

				else = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = IBR_SPAIN
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_spain = yes }

					formable_decision_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_visual } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = form_spain_affected_states_tt
				formable_decision_effect_tooltip = yes
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected }

					is_spain = yes
				}
				else = {
					required_states_to_form_spain = yes
				}
			}
		}

		cost = global.formables_cost_50?50

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5000
		}
	}

			}

			clr_country_flag = can_form_JAP_UNITED
			clr_country_flag = can_form_USA_WEST

				limit = { can_form_rapa_nui = yes }

				set_country_flag = can_form_SOA_UNITED
			}
			set_country_flag = can_form_OCE_UNITED
			set_country_flag = can_form_ASI_UNITED

			set_cosmetic_tag = PLY_UNITED

				every_state = {
					limit = { is_polynesia = yes }

					formable_decision_effect = yes
				}
			}

				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_visual } }

				formable_decision_effect_tooltip = yes
			}
		}

				}
				else = {
					required_states_to_form_polynesia = yes

			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision form_balochistan"
			set_country_flag = can_form_PER_UNITED
			set_country_flag = can_form_PAK_UNITED

			if = {
				limit = { original_tag = NIZ }

				set_cosmetic_tag = PER_BALOCHISTAN_KALAT

				else = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = PER_BALOCHISTAN
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_balochistan = yes }

					formable_decision_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_visual } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = form_balochistan_affected_states_tt
				formable_decision_effect_tooltip = yes
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected }

					is_balochistan = yes
				}
				else = {
					required_states_to_form_balochistan = yes
				}
			}
		}

		cost = global.formables_cost_25?25

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5000
		}
	}

			clr_country_flag = can_form_AFR_UNITED

			set_country_flag = can_form_EAR_UNITED

			set_cosmetic_tag = MEA_UNITED

			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_middle_east = yes }

					formable_decision_effect = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = formables_visual } }

				custom_effect_tooltip = form_middle_east_affected_states_tt
				formable_decision_effect_tooltip = yes
			}
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_flag = formables_highlight_affected }

					is_middle_east = yes
				}
				else = {
					required_states_to_form_middle_east = yes
				}
			}
		}

		cost = global.formables_cost_200?200

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5000
		}
	}

	form_earth = {
		icon = generic_form_nation
		allowed = {
			always = yes
		}
		visible = {
			has_cosmetics_to_form_earth = yes
		}
		available = {
			has_states_to_form_earth = yes
		}
		complete_effect = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Decision form_earth"
			set_country_flag = formed_EAR_UNITED

			clr_country_flag = can_form_EAR_UNITED

			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader_ideology = anarchism }

				set_cosmetic_tag = EAR_UNITED_ANARCHIST

				else = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = EAR_UNITED
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					formable_decision_effect = yes
				}
			}
			formable_decision_effect_tooltip_default = yes
		}

		highlight_states = {
			highlight_states_trigger = {
				always = yes
			}
		}

		cost = global.formables_cost_300?300

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 5000
		}
	}
}
